(******************************************************************************************

 Whiskering of transformations of enriched profunctors

 We define the whiskering operations for transformations of enriched profunctors. The
 constructions and proofs boil down to calculations with coends. To construct the desired
 morphisms, we use the mapping property and to prove the necessary laws, we use the
 uniqueness of such morphisms.

 Content
 1. Right whiskering
 2. Left whiskering

 ******************************************************************************************)
Require Import UniMath.Foundations.All.

(** * 1. Right whiskering *)
Section RightWhiskering.
  Context {V : benabou_cosmos}
          {C₁ C₂ C₃ : category}
          {E₁ : enrichment C₁ V}
          {E₂ : enrichment C₂ V}
          {E₃ : enrichment C₃ V}
          {P₁ P₂ : E₁ ↛e E₂}
          (τ : enriched_profunctor_transformation P₁ P₂)
          (Q : E₂ ↛e E₃).

  
V: benabou_cosmos
C₁, C₂, C₃: category
E₁: enrichment C₁ V
E₂: enrichment C₂ V
E₃: enrichment C₃ V
P₁, P₂: enriched_profunctor E₁ E₂
τ: enriched_profunctor_transformation P₁ P₂
Q: enriched_profunctor E₂ E₃
z: C₃
y₁, y₂: C₂
x: C₁
lmap_e P₁ y₂ y₁ x #⊗ identity (Q z y₁)
· (τ y₁ x #⊗ identity (Q z y₁)
   · comp_enriched_profunctor_in P₂ Q z x y₁) =
sym_mon_braiding V (E₂ ⦃ y₁, y₂ ⦄) (P₁ y₂ x)
#⊗ identity (Q z y₁)
· mon_lassociator (P₁ y₂ x) (E₂ ⦃ y₁, y₂ ⦄) (Q z y₁)
· identity (P₁ y₂ x) #⊗ rmap_e Q z y₁ y₂
· (τ y₂ x #⊗ identity (Q z y₂)
   · comp_enriched_profunctor_in P₂ Q z x y₂)

· identity (P₁ y₂ x) #⊗ rmap_e Q z y₁ y₂
· (τ y₂ x #⊗ identity (Q z y₂)
   · comp_enriched_profunctor_in P₂ Q z x y₂)

      · (τ y₂ x #⊗ identity (Q z y₂)

· τ y₂ x #⊗ identity (Q z y₂)
· comp_enriched_profunctor_in P₂ Q z x y₂

V: benabou_cosmos
C₁, C₂, C₃: category
E₁: enrichment C₁ V
E₂: enrichment C₂ V
E₃: enrichment C₃ V
P₁, P₂: enriched_profunctor E₁ E₂
τ: enriched_profunctor_transformation P₁ P₂
Q: enriched_profunctor E₂ E₃
z: C₃
y₁, y₂: C₂
x: C₁
sym_mon_braiding V (E₂ ⦃ y₁, y₂ ⦄) (P₁ y₂ x)
#⊗ identity (Q z y₁)
· (mon_lassociator (P₁ y₂ x) (E₂ ⦃ y₁, y₂ ⦄) (Q z y₁)
   · (τ y₂ x #⊗ identity ((E₂ ⦃ y₁, y₂ ⦄) ⊗ Q z y₁)
      · identity (P₂ y₂ x) #⊗ rmap_e Q z y₁ y₂)) =
(identity (E₂ ⦃ y₁, y₂ ⦄) #⊗ τ y₂ x)
#⊗ identity (Q z y₁)
· mon_lassociator (E₂ ⦃ y₁, y₂ ⦄) (P₂ y₂ x) (Q z y₁)
· sym_mon_braiding V (E₂ ⦃ y₁, y₂ ⦄)
    (P₂ y₂ x ⊗ Q z y₁)
· mon_lassociator (P₂ y₂ x) (Q z y₁) (E₂ ⦃ y₁, y₂ ⦄)
· identity (P₂ y₂ x)
  #⊗ (sym_mon_braiding V (Q z y₁) (E₂ ⦃ y₁, y₂ ⦄)
      · rmap_e Q z y₁ y₂)

    
V: benabou_cosmos
C₁, C₂, C₃: category
E₁: enrichment C₁ V
E₂: enrichment C₂ V
E₃: enrichment C₃ V
P₁, P₂: enriched_profunctor E₁ E₂
τ: enriched_profunctor_transformation P₁ P₂
Q: enriched_profunctor E₂ E₃
z: C₃
y₁, y₂: C₂
x: C₁
sym_mon_braiding V (E₂ ⦃ y₁, y₂ ⦄) (P₁ y₂ x)
#⊗ identity (Q z y₁)
· (mon_lassociator (P₁ y₂ x) (E₂ ⦃ y₁, y₂ ⦄) (Q z y₁)
   · (τ y₂ x #⊗ identity ((E₂ ⦃ y₁, y₂ ⦄) ⊗ Q z y₁)
      · identity (P₂ y₂ x) #⊗ rmap_e Q z y₁ y₂)) =
(identity (E₂ ⦃ y₁, y₂ ⦄) #⊗ τ y₂ x)
#⊗ identity (Q z y₁)

lmap_e P₁ y₂ y₁ x #⊗ identity (Q z y₁) · ?fs y₁ =

#⊗ identity (Q z y₁)
· mon_lassociator (P₁ y₂ x) (E₂ ⦃ y₁, y₂ ⦄) (Q z y₁)

   · comp_enriched_profunctor_in P₂ Q z x y₁) =

   · comp_enriched_profunctor_in P₂ Q z x y₂)

      exact (rwhisker_enriched_profunctor_mor_eq z y₁ y₂ x).
  Defined.

     τ y x #⊗ identity (Q z y)
     · comp_enriched_profunctor_in P₂ Q z x y)

    apply idpath.

  #⊗ identity (E₃ ⦃ z₂, z₁ ⦄)
· internal_eval (E₃ ⦃ z₂, z₁ ⦄)
    (comp_enriched_profunctor_ob P₂ Q z₂ x) =
comp_enriched_profunctor_in P₁ Q z₁ x y #⊗ h
· internal_transpose
    (identity (E₃ ⦃ z₂, z₁ ⦄)
     #⊗ comp_enriched_profunctor_lmap P₁ Q z₁ z₂ x
     · sym_mon_braiding V (E₃ ⦃ z₂, z₁ ⦄)
         ((E₃ ⦃ z₂, z₁ ⦄)
          ⊸ comp_enriched_profunctor_ob P₁ Q z₂ x)
     · internal_eval (E₃ ⦃ z₂, z₁ ⦄)
         (comp_enriched_profunctor_ob P₁ Q z₂ x)
     · rwhisker_enriched_profunctor_mor z₂ x)
  #⊗ identity (E₃ ⦃ z₂, z₁ ⦄)
· internal_eval (E₃ ⦃ z₂, z₁ ⦄)
    (comp_enriched_profunctor_ob P₂ Q z₂ x)

      #⊗ comp_enriched_profunctor_lmap P₂ Q z₁ z₂ x

           ((E₃ ⦃ z₂, z₁ ⦄)
            ⊸ comp_enriched_profunctor_ob P₂ Q z₂ x)
         · internal_eval (E₃ ⦃ z₂, z₁ ⦄)
             (comp_enriched_profunctor_ob P₂ Q z₂ x)))) =
identity (E₃ ⦃ z₂, z₁ ⦄)
#⊗ comp_enriched_profunctor_in P₁ Q z₁ x y
· (identity (E₃ ⦃ z₂, z₁ ⦄)
   #⊗ comp_enriched_profunctor_lmap P₁ Q z₁ z₂ x
   · (sym_mon_braiding V (E₃ ⦃ z₂, z₁ ⦄)
        ((E₃ ⦃ z₂, z₁ ⦄)
         ⊸ comp_enriched_profunctor_ob P₁ Q z₂ x)
      · (internal_eval (E₃ ⦃ z₂, z₁ ⦄)
           (comp_enriched_profunctor_ob P₁ Q z₂ x)
         · rwhisker_enriched_profunctor_mor z₂ x)))

   #⊗ identity (E₁ ⦃ x₁, x₂ ⦄)
   · (internal_transpose
        (identity (E₁ ⦃ x₁, x₂ ⦄)
         #⊗ rwhisker_enriched_profunctor_mor z x₁
         · (identity (E₁ ⦃ x₁, x₂ ⦄)
            #⊗ comp_enriched_profunctor_rmap P₂ Q z x₁
                 x₂
            · (sym_mon_braiding V (E₁ ⦃ x₁, x₂ ⦄)
                 ((E₁ ⦃ x₁, x₂ ⦄)
                  ⊸ comp_enriched_profunctor_ob P₂ Q z
                      x₂)
               · internal_eval (E₁ ⦃ x₁, x₂ ⦄)
                   (comp_enriched_profunctor_ob P₂ Q z
                      x₂))))
      #⊗ identity (E₁ ⦃ x₁, x₂ ⦄)
      · internal_eval (E₁ ⦃ x₁, x₂ ⦄)
          (comp_enriched_profunctor_ob P₂ Q z x₂))) =

· (comp_enriched_profunctor_in P₁ Q z x₁ y
   #⊗ identity (E₁ ⦃ x₁, x₂ ⦄)
   · (internal_transpose
        (identity (E₁ ⦃ x₁, x₂ ⦄)
         #⊗ comp_enriched_profunctor_rmap P₁ Q z x₁ x₂

          (comp_enriched_profunctor_ob P₂ Q z x₂)))

 · comp_enriched_profunctor_rmap P₁ Q z x₁ x₂)
#⊗ identity (E₁ ⦃ x₁, x₂ ⦄)
· internal_eval (E₁ ⦃ x₁, x₂ ⦄)
    (comp_enriched_profunctor_ob P₁ Q z x₂)
· rwhisker_enriched_profunctor_mor z x₂ =
sym_mon_braiding V (P₁ y x₁ ⊗ Q z y) (E₁ ⦃ x₁, x₂ ⦄)
· (mon_rassociator (E₁ ⦃ x₁, x₂ ⦄) (P₁ y x₁) (Q z y)
   · ((identity (E₁ ⦃ x₁, x₂ ⦄) #⊗ τ y x₁
       · rmap_e P₂ y x₁ x₂) #⊗ identity (Q z y)
      · comp_enriched_profunctor_in P₂ Q z x₂ y))

(** * 2. Left whiskering *)
Section LeftWhiskering.
  Context {V : benabou_cosmos}
          {C₁ C₂ C₃ : category}
          {E₁ : enrichment C₁ V}
          {E₂ : enrichment C₂ V}
          {E₃ : enrichment C₃ V}
          (P : E₁ ↛e E₂)
          {Q₁ Q₂ : E₂ ↛e E₃}
          (τ : enriched_profunctor_transformation Q₁ Q₂).

  
V: benabou_cosmos
C₁, C₂, C₃: category
E₁: enrichment C₁ V
E₂: enrichment C₂ V
E₃: enrichment C₃ V
P: enriched_profunctor E₁ E₂
Q₁, Q₂: enriched_profunctor E₂ E₃
τ: enriched_profunctor_transformation Q₁ Q₂
z: C₃
y₁, y₂: C₂
x: C₁
lmap_e P y₂ y₁ x #⊗ identity (Q₁ z y₁)
· (identity (P y₁ x) #⊗ τ z y₁
   · comp_enriched_profunctor_in P Q₂ z x y₁) =
sym_mon_braiding V (E₂ ⦃ y₁, y₂ ⦄) (P y₂ x)
#⊗ identity (Q₁ z y₁)
· mon_lassociator (P y₂ x) (E₂ ⦃ y₁, y₂ ⦄) (Q₁ z y₁)
· identity (P y₂ x) #⊗ rmap_e Q₁ z y₁ y₂
· (identity (P y₂ x) #⊗ τ z y₂
   · comp_enriched_profunctor_in P Q₂ z x y₂)

   · identity (P y₂ x)
     #⊗ (identity (E₂ ⦃ y₁, y₂ ⦄) #⊗ τ z y₁)) = ?y'

   · (sym_mon_braiding V (P y₂ x ⊗ Q₂ z y₁)
        (E₂ ⦃ y₁, y₂ ⦄)
      · mon_rassociator (E₂ ⦃ y₁, y₂ ⦄) (P y₂ x)
          (Q₂ z y₁))) = ?b

    ((E₃ ⦃ z₂, z₁ ⦄)
     ⊸ comp_enriched_profunctor_ob P Q₁ z₂ x)

      · (identity (E₁ ⦃ x₁, x₂ ⦄)
         #⊗ comp_enriched_profunctor_rmap P Q₂ z x₁ x₂
         · sym_mon_braiding V (E₁ ⦃ x₁, x₂ ⦄)

             (comp_enriched_profunctor_ob P Q₂ z x₂))))

τ: enriched_profunctor_transformation Q₁ Q₂
z: C₃
x₁, x₂: C₁
y: C₂
sym_mon_braiding V (P y x₁ ⊗ Q₁ z y) (E₁ ⦃ x₁, x₂ ⦄)
· identity (E₁ ⦃ x₁, x₂ ⦄)
  #⊗ comp_enriched_profunctor_in P Q₁ z x₁ y
· identity (E₁ ⦃ x₁, x₂ ⦄)
  #⊗ lwhisker_enriched_profunctor_mor z x₁
· identity (E₁ ⦃ x₁, x₂ ⦄)
  #⊗ comp_enriched_profunctor_rmap P Q₂ z x₁ x₂
· sym_mon_braiding V (E₁ ⦃ x₁, x₂ ⦄)
    ((E₁ ⦃ x₁, x₂ ⦄)
     ⊸ comp_enriched_profunctor_ob P Q₂ z x₂)
· internal_eval (E₁ ⦃ x₁, x₂ ⦄)
    (comp_enriched_profunctor_ob P Q₂ z x₂) =

  #⊗ comp_enriched_profunctor_rmap P Q₁ z x₁ x₂

    ((E₁ ⦃ x₁, x₂ ⦄)
     ⊸ comp_enriched_profunctor_ob P Q₁ z x₂)
· internal_eval (E₁ ⦃ x₁, x₂ ⦄)
    (comp_enriched_profunctor_ob P Q₁ z x₂)
· lwhisker_enriched_profunctor_mor z x₂

· rmap_e P y x₁ x₂ #⊗ identity (Q₂ z y)
· comp_enriched_profunctor_in P Q₂ z x₂ y = ?b
